FIXED    (agent remediation succeeded)\n    13→                  |\n    14→PENDING ----+---> FAILED   (agent remediation failed / timed out / rollback triggered)\n    15→                  |\n    16→ | Terminal? |\n    24→|--------|-------|-------------|-----------|\n    25→| PENDING | `\"PENDING\"` | Finding parsed from validation report; awaiting remediation | No |\n    26→| FIXED | `\"FIXED\"` | Remediation agent successfully applied fix; certify step confirms | Yes |\n    27→| FAILED | `\"FAILED\"` | Remediation agent failed, timed out, or rollback was triggered | Yes |\n    28→| SKIPPED | `\"SKIPPED\"` | Finding excluded from remediation by filter or classification | Yes |\n    29→\n    30→---\n    31→\n    32→## Transition Rules\n    33→\n    34→### Valid Transitions\n    35→\n    36→| From | To | Trigger | Phase |\n    37→|------|----|---------|-------|\n    38→| PENDING | FIXED | Agent completes successfully; output passes verification | Phase 3 (Remediation Execution) |\n    39→| PENDING | FAILED | Agent exits non-zero, times out, or rollback is triggered | Phase 3 (Remediation Execution) |\n    40→| PENDING | SKIPPED | Finding filtered by scope selection (option 1/2/3) | - Findings with `agreement_category == \"NO_ACTION_REQUIRED\"` -> `SKIPPED`\n    58→   - Findings with `agreement_category == \"OUT_OF_SCOPE\"` -> `SKIPPED`\n    59→   - Findings outside the user's scope selection (option 1: BLOCKING only, option 2: BLOCKING+WARNING) -> `SKIPPED`\n    60→3. **Zero-findings guard**: If 0 actionable findings remain after filtering, all findings are `SKIPPED` and D-0003: Finding Lifecycle Model\n\n## Overview\n\nCanonical finding status lifecycle for the v2.22 remediate/certify pipeline extension. Defines valid statuses, transitions, terminal states, and initial state assignment rules.\n\n---\n\n## State Machine\n\n```\n                  +---> FIXED    (agent remediation succeeded)\n                  |\nPENDING ----+---> FAILED   (agent remediation failed / timed out / rollback triggered)\n                  |\n                  +---> SKIPPED  (filtered out / NO_ACTION_REQUIRED / OUT_OF_SCOPE)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Status Definitions\n\n| Status | Value | Description | Terminal? |\n|--------|-------|-------------|-----------|\n| PENDING | `\"PENDING\"` | Finding parsed from validation report; awaiting remediation | No |\n| FIXED | `\"FIXED\"` | Remediation agent successfully applied fix; certify step confirms | Yes |\n| FAILED | `\"FAILED\"` | Remediation agent failed, timed out, or rollback was triggered | Yes |\n| SKIPPED | `\"SKIPPED\"` | Finding excluded from remediation by filter or classification | Yes |\n\n---\n\n## Transition Rules\n\n### Valid Transitions\n\n| From | To | Trigger | Phase |\n|------|----|---------|-------|\n| PENDING | FIXED | Agent completes successfully; output passes verification | Phase 3 (Remediation Execution) |\n| PENDING | FAILED | Agent exits non-zero, times out, or rollback is triggered | Phase 3 (Remediation Execution) |\n| PENDING | SKIPPED | Finding filtered by scope selection (option 1/2/3) | Phase 2 (Prompt & Filter) |\n| PENDING | SKIPPED | Finding classified as NO_ACTION_REQUIRED | Phase 2 (Prompt & Filter) |\n| PENDING | SKIPPED | Finding classified as OUT_OF_SCOPE | Phase 2 (Prompt & Filter) |\n\n### Invalid Transitions (Enforced)\n\n- FIXED -> any: terminal state, no further transitions\n- FAILED -> any: terminal state, no further transitions\n- SKIPPED -> any: terminal state, no further transitions\n- Any -> PENDING: initial state only, never re-assigned\n\n---\n\n## Initial State Assignment\n\n1. **Parser output**: All findings parsed from validation reports are assigned `status = PENDING`\n2. **Immediate SKIP**: During Phase 2 filtering:\n   - Findings with `agreement_category == \"NO_ACTION_REQUIRED\"` -> `SKIPPED`\n   - Findings with `agreement_category == \"OUT_OF_SCOPE\"` -> `SKIPPED`\n   - Findings outside the user's scope selection (option 1: BLOCKING only, option 2: BLOCKING+WARNING) -> `SKIPPED`\n3. **Zero-findings guard**: If 0 actionable findings remain after filtering, all findings are `SKIPPED` and pipeline proceeds to certify with stub tasklist\n\n---\n\n## Scenario Coverage\n\n### Scenario 1: Filtering (Phase 2)\n- User selects Option 1 (BLOCKING only)\n- WARNING and INFO findings -> `SKIPPED`\n- BLOCKING findings remain `PENDING` for remediation\n\n### Scenario 2: Successful Remediation (Phase 3)\n- Agent receives finding with `status = PENDING`\n- Agent modifies target files successfully\n- Output passes basic verification\n- Finding -> `FIXED`\n\n### Scenario 3: Failed Remediation (Phase 3)\n- Agent receives finding with `status = PENDING`\n- Agent exits non-zero or times out\n- Snapshot rollback triggers (`.pre-remediate` files restored)\n- Finding -> `FAILED`\n\n### Scenario 4: Rollback-Triggered Failure (Phase 3)\n- Agent modifies files but introduces errors\n- Post-remediation check detects issues\n- Rollback to `.pre-remediate` snapshot\n- Finding -> `FAILED`\n\n### Scenario 5: Skip Remediation Path (Phase 2)\n- User selects option `n` (skip remediation)\n- All PENDING findings -> remain `PENDING` (state saved as `validated-with-issues`)\n- No transition occurs; pipeline ends without remediation\n\n### Scenario 6: Zero Actionable Findings (Phase 2)\n- All findings are NO_ACTION_REQUIRED or OUT_OF_SCOPE\n- All findings -> `SKIPPED`\n- Stub tasklist generated (`actionable: 0`)\n- Pipeline proceeds to certify\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Notes\n\n### Finding Dataclass Field\n```python\nstatus: str = \"PENDING\"  # One of: PENDING, FIXED, FAILED, SKIPPED\n```\n\n### Tasklist Representation\n- `remediation-tasklist.md` records each finding with its status\n- Pre-execution: all actionable findings show `PENDING`, filtered findings show `SKIPPED`\n- Post-execution: updated in-place with `FIXED` or `FAILED` outcomes\n\n### State File Integration\n- Finding statuses are summarized in `.roadmap-state.json` under the `remediate` key\n- Summary counts: `{fixed: N, failed: N, skipped: N, total: N}`\n- Individual finding statuses stored in the tasklist artifact, not in the state file\n\n---\n\n## Alignment with Existing Pipeline Patterns\n\nThe finding lifecycle intentionally mirrors the existing `StepStatus` enum in `pipeline/models.py`:\n- `StepStatus.PASS` ~ `Finding.FIXED` (success)\n- `StepStatus.FAIL` / `StepStatus.TIMEOUT` ~ `Finding.FAILED` (failure)\n- `StepStatus.SKIPPED` ~ `Finding.SKIPPED` (not executed)\n- `StepStatus.PENDING` ~ `Finding.PENDING` (awaiting execution)\n\nThis alignment ensures conceptual consistency across the pipeline.\n","numLines":130,"startLine":1,"totalLines":130}}}

Builds steps via `_build_steps()`\n    51→  2. Handles `--dry-run` and `--resume`\n    52→  3. Delegates to `execute_pipeline()` with `roadmap_run_step` as the StepRunner\n    53→  4. Saves state via `_save_state()`\n    54→  5. Auto-invokes validation via `_auto_invoke_validate()`\n    55→\n    56→### Extension Points for New Steps\n    57→- New steps (remediate, certify) can be added to the `_build_steps()` return list\n    58→- `execute_roadmap()` already handles post-pipeline actions (validation) -- remediation can follow the same pattern\n    59→- The interactive prompt (FR-003, FR-032) should live in `execute_roadmap()`, NOT in `execute_pipeline()`, preserving the latter's non-interactive contract\n    60→\n    61→### State Preservation\n    62→- `_save_state()` preserves existing `validation` and `fidelity_status` keys across rewrites\n    63→- New keys (e.g., `remediate`, `certify`) can be added additively without breaking backward compatibility\n    64→\n    65→---\n    66→\n    67→## 3. validate_executor.py -- ClaudeProcess Patterns\n    68→\n    69→**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_executor.py`\n    70→\n    71→### Agent Spawning Pattern\n    72→- `validate_run_step()` mirrors `roadmap_run_step()`: builds argv, launches ClaudeProcess, waits with timeout, sanitizes output\n    73→- Both use the same `ClaudeProcess` API with identical parameter patterns:\n    74→  - `prompt`, `output_file`, `error_file`, `max_turns`, `model`, `permission_flag`, `timeout_seconds`, `output_format`, `extra_args`\n    75→- Inline embedding pattern: read input files into prompt string (up to 100KB), fall back to `--file` flags for larger inputs\n    76→\n    77→### Multi-Agent Parallel Execution\n    78→- `_build_multi_agent_steps()`: creates N parallel reflection steps (one per agent), then a sequential adversarial-merge step\n    79→- The parallel group pattern is: `[reflect_steps, merge_step]` -- parallel reflections followed by sequential merge\n    80→- **Precedent for remediation**: This is the exact pattern needed for parallel remediation agents (one per finding/file batch)"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"7adace0d-ab39-41a6-9bfa-16fcab0e76c7","uuid":"80406fb5-66bf-44f1-8bf9-270471407565","tool_use_result":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.dev/releases/current/v2.22-RoadmapRemediate/artifacts/D-0001/notes.md","content":"# D-0001: Pipeline Foundation Review Notes\n\n## Overview\n\nReview of the existing pipeline infrastructure to confirm extension points, state schema, and patterns available for v2.22 remediate/certify steps.\n\n---\n\n## 1. execute_pipeline() Step Model\n\n**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/executor.py`\n\n### Step Sequencing\n- `execute_pipeline()` accepts `steps: list[Step | list[Step]]` -- a mixed list where:\n  - Single `Step` entries execute sequentially\n  - `list[Step]` entries execute as parallel groups (all steps in the group run concurrently via threads)\n- For each step: `on_step_start` -> `run_step()` -> gate check -> `on_step_complete` -> `on_state_update`\n- If any step fails after retry exhaustion: pipeline HALTs (no further steps execute)\n- Parallel groups: if any step in the group fails, remaining steps are cancelled via `threading.Event`\n\n### Retry Logic\n- `retry_limit` on `Step` dataclass controls retries (retry_limit=1 means 2 total attempts)\n- Retry only happens when gate check fails; subprocess errors (non-zero exit, timeout) are terminal\n\n### Gate Evaluation\n- Two modes: `GateMode.BLOCKING` (synchronous, default) and `GateMode.TRAILING` (deferred, grace period)\n- `grace_period == 0` forces BLOCKING regardless of step's `gate_mode`\n- Trailing gates collect at sync point after all steps complete\n\n### State Save Pattern\n- `_build_state()` produces a dict with `steps`, `total`, `passed`, `failed` counts\n- Called via `on_state_update` callback after each step/group completes\n- Consumers (roadmap, sprint) provide their own `on_state_update` implementation\n\n### Extension Points\n- **StepRunner Protocol**: Any callable matching `(Step, PipelineConfig, Callable[[], bool]) -> StepResult`\n- **Callbacks**: `on_step_start`, `on_step_complete`, `on_state_update`, `cancel_check`\n- **TrailingGateRunner**: Optional trailing gate support\n\n---\n\n## 2. execute_roadmap() Extension Points\n\n**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/executor.py`\n\n### Pipeline Composition\n- `_build_steps()` constructs a 9-step pipeline (8 sequential + 1 parallel group for generate)\n- Steps: extract -> [generate-A, generate-B] -> diff -> debate -> score -> merge -> test-strategy -> spec-fidelity\n- `execute_roadmap()` is the top-level orchestrator that:\n  1. Builds steps via `_build_steps()`\n  2. Handles `--dry-run` and `--resume`\n  3. Delegates to `execute_pipeline()` with `roadmap_run_step` as the StepRunner\n  4. Saves state via `_save_state()`\n  5. Auto-invokes validation via `_auto_invoke_validate()`\n\n### Extension Points for New Steps\n- New steps (remediate, certify) can be added to the `_build_steps()` return list\n- `execute_roadmap()` already handles post-pipeline actions (validation) -- remediation can follow the same pattern\n- The interactive prompt (FR-003, FR-032) should live in `execute_roadmap()`, NOT in `execute_pipeline()`, preserving the latter's non-interactive contract\n\n### State Preservation\n- `_save_state()` preserves existing `validation` and `fidelity_status` keys across rewrites\n- New keys (e.g., `remediate`, `certify`) can be added additively without breaking backward compatibility\n\n---\n\n## 3. validate_executor.py -- ClaudeProcess Patterns\n\n**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_executor.py`\n\n### Agent Spawning Pattern\n- `validate_run_step()` mirrors `roadmap_run_step()`: builds argv, launches ClaudeProcess, waits with timeout, sanitizes output\n- Both use the same `ClaudeProcess` API with identical parameter patterns:\n  - `prompt`, `output_file`, `error_file`, `max_turns`, `model`, `permission_flag`, `timeout_seconds`, `output_format`, `extra_args`\n- Inline embedding pattern: read input files into prompt string (up to 100KB), fall back to `--file` flags for larger inputs\n\n### Multi-Agent Parallel Execution\n- `_build_multi_agent_steps()`: creates N parallel reflection steps (one per agent), then a sequential adversarial-merge step\n- The parallel group pattern is: `[reflect_steps, merge_step]` -- parallel reflections followed by sequential merge\n- **Precedent for remediation**: This is the exact pattern needed for parallel remediation agents (one per finding/file batch)","numLines":80,"startLine":1,"totalLines":196}}}

The new `remediate` and `certify` step entries will be written by new step-specific code (Phases 3-5) using the same `_save_state()` pattern. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_012jY91PLue8QrsoJane5rj4","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_015skUh7CkUKzrxtkLixB8C6","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/remediate_parser.py","content":"\"\"\"Parser for validation reports -- extracts Finding objects.\n\nProvides two pure functions:\n- parse_validation_report(text) -> list[Finding]  (primary: merged reports)\n- parse_individual_reports(report_texts) -> list[Finding]  (fallback: with dedup)\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\n\nfrom .models import Finding\n\n# Severity ordering for deduplication (higher index wins)\n_SEVERITY_RANK = {\"INFO\": 0, \"WARNING\": 1, \"BLOCKING\": 2}\n\n\ndef parse_validation_report(text: str) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Parse a merged validation report into Finding objects.\n\n    Supports two merged report formats:\n    1. reflect-merged.md -- has Agreement Table with Remediation Status column\n       and Consolidated Findings sections\n    2. merged-validation-report.md -- has Agreement Table (no Remediation Status)\n       and Consolidated Findings sections\n\n    Both share the Consolidated Findings structure with BLOCKING/WARNING/INFO\n    subsections containing structured finding blocks.\n\n    This is a pure function: no I/O, no subprocess calls, no side effects.\n\n    Raises ValueError if no findings could be extracted.\n    \"\"\"\n    findings = _parse_consolidated_findings(text)\n    if not findings:\n        findings = _parse_flat_findings(text)\n    if not findings:\n        raise ValueError(\n            \"No findings extracted from report. \"\n            \"Expected '## Consolidated Findings' or '## Findings' section \"\n            \"with structured finding blocks.\"\n        )\n    # Overlay agreement categories from the Agreement Table if present\n    _overlay_agreement_categories(text, findings)\n    # Overlay remediation status from Agreement Table if present\n    _overlay_remediation_status(text, findings)\n    return findings\n\n\ndef parse_individual_reports(report_texts: list[str]) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Parse multiple individual reflect-*.md reports with deduplication.\n\n    Deduplication rule (spec §8/OQ-003):\n    1. Location match: same file + within 5 lines = candidate duplicate\n    2. Severity resolution: higher severity wins (BLOCKING > WARNING > INFO)\n    3. Fix guidance: merged from both reports\n\n    Non-matching findings included as-is from their source report.\n\n    This is a pure function: no I/O, no subprocess calls, no side effects.\n    \"\"\"\n    all_findings: list[Finding] = []\n    for text in report_texts:\n        try:\n            findings = _parse_flat_findings(text)\n            if not findings:\n                findings = _parse_consolidated_findings(text)\n            all_findings.extend(findings)\n        except ValueError:\n            continue\n\n    if not all_findings:\n        return []\n\n    return _deduplicate_findings(all_findings)\n\n\ndef _parse_consolidated_findings(text: str) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Extract findings from '## Consolidated Findings' sections.\"\"\"\n    # Find the Consolidated Findings section\n    match = re.search(r\"^## Consolidated Findings\\s*$\", text, re.MULTILINE)\n    if not match:\n        return []\n\n    section_text = text[match.end():]\n    # Truncate at next H2\n    next_h2 = re.search(r\"^## \", section_text, re.MULTILINE)\n    if next_h2:\n        section_text = section_text[:next_h2.start()]\n\n    return _extract_finding_blocks(section_text)\n\n\ndef _parse_flat_findings(text: str) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Extract findings from individual report '## Findings' sections.\"\"\"\n    match = re.search(r\"^## Findings\\s*$\", text, re.MULTILINE)\n    if not match:\n        return []\n\n    section_text = text[match.end():]\n    next_h2 = re.search(r\"^## \", section_text, re.MULTILINE)\n    if next_h2:\n        section_text = section_text[:next_h2.start()]\n\n    return _extract_finding_blocks(section_text)\n\n\ndef _extract_finding_blocks(section_text: str) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Extract individual finding blocks from a findings section.\n\n    Supports two patterns:\n    1. Bold header: **[F-XX] [SEVERITY] Dimension: Description**\n    2. Bold header: **[SEVERITY] Dimension**: Description\n    \"\"\"\n    findings: list[Finding] = []\n\n    # Pattern 1: **[F-XX] [SEVERITY] Dimension: Description**\n    # Pattern 2: **F-XX [SEVERITY] Dimension: Description** (variant without brackets on ID)\n    # Also matches: - **[SEVERITY] Dimension**: Description (individual reports)\n    finding_pattern = re.compile(\n        r\"[-*]*\\s*\\*\\*\"\n        r\"(?:\\[?(F-\\d+)\\]?\\s+)?\"          # Optional finding ID\n        r\"\\[(BLOCKING|WARNING|INFO)\\]\\s+\"   # Severity (required)\n        r\"([^:*]+)\"                         # Dimension\n        r\"[:\\s]*\"                           # Separator\n        r\"([^*]+)?\"                         # Description (optional inline)\n        r\"\\*\\*\",\n        re.IGNORECASE,\n    )\n\n    blocks = list(finding_pattern.finditer(section_text))\n\n    for i, block_match in enumerate(blocks):\n        block_start = block_match.end()\n        block_end = blocks[i + 1].start() if i + 1 < len(blocks) else len(section_text)\n        block_body = section_text[block_start:block_end]\n\n        finding_id = block_match.group(1) or f\"F-{len(findings) + 1:02d}\"\n        severity = block_match.group(2).upper()\n        dimension = block_match.group(3).strip().rstrip(\":\")\n        description = (block_match.group(4) or \"\").strip()\n\n        # If description is empty, use the full matched text\n        if not description:\n            description = f\"{dimension}\"\n\n        location = _extract_field(block_body, \"Location\")\n        evidence = _extract_field(block_body, \"Evidence\")\n        fix_guidance = _extract_field(block_body, \"Fix guidance\")\n        agreement = _extract_field(block_body, \"Agreement\")\n\n        # Validate required fields\n        _validate_required_fields(finding_id, severity, description)\n\n        files_affected = _extract_files_from_location(location)\n\n        findings.append(Finding(\n            id=finding_id,\n            severity=severity,\n            dimension=dimension,\n            description=description,\n            location=location,\n            evidence=evidence,\n            fix_guidance=fix_guidance,\n            files_affected=files_affected,\n            status=\"PENDING\",\n            agreement_category=agreement,\n        ))\n\n    return findings\n\n\ndef _extract_field(body: str, field_name: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Extract a field value from a finding block body.\n\n    Handles multi-line values that continue with indentation.\n    \"\"\"\n    pattern = re.compile(\n        rf\"^\\s*-\\s+{field_name}\\s*:\\s*(.+?)(?=\\n\\s*-\\s+\\w|\\n\\s*\\n\\*\\*|\\Z)\",\n        re.MULTILINE | re.DOTALL,\n    )\n    match = pattern.search(body)\n    if not match:\n        return \"\"\n    # Clean up the extracted text\n    raw = match.group(1).strip()\n    # Collapse continuation lines\n    lines = raw.split(\"\\n\")\n    cleaned = []\n    for line in lines:\n        stripped = line.strip()\n        if stripped.startswith(\"- \") and cleaned:\n            # Sub-bullet -- keep as-is\n            cleaned.append(stripped)\n        elif stripped:\n            cleaned.append(stripped)\n    return \" \".join(cleaned) if len(cleaned) <= 2 else \"\\n\".join(cleaned)\n\n\ndef _extract_files_from_location(location: str) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract file paths from a location string like 'roadmap.md:23, 359-363'.\"\"\"\n    if not location:\n        return []\n    # Match patterns like filename.ext, path/filename.ext\n    file_pattern = re.compile(r\"`?([a-zA-Z0-9_./-]+\\.[a-zA-Z0-9]+)(?::\\d+[^`]*)?`?\")\n    matches = file_pattern.findall(location)\n    # Deduplicate while preserving order\n    seen: set[str] = set()\n    result: list[str] = []\n    for f in matches:\n        if f not in seen:\n            seen.add(f)\n            result.append(f)\n    return result\n\n\ndef _validate_required_fields(\n    finding_id: str, severity: str, description: str\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Validate that required structured fields are present.\n\n    Raises ValueError when required fields are absent.\n    \"\"\"\n    missing = []\n    if not finding_id:\n        missing.append(\"id\")\n    if not severity:\n        missing.append(\"severity\")\n    if not description:\n        missing.append(\"description\")\n    if missing:\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"Required finding fields missing: {', '.join(missing)}. \"\n            \"Cannot parse finding without id, severity, and description.\"\n        )\n\n\ndef _overlay_agreement_categories(text: str, findings: list[Finding]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Overlay agreement_category from Agreement Table onto findings.\"\"\"\n    # Match Agreement Table rows: | F-XX... | ... | ... | CATEGORY |\n    table_pattern = re.compile(\n        r\"\\|\\s*(F-\\d+)[^|]*\\|\"   # Finding ID column\n        r\"[^|]*\\|\"               # Agent A or Description column\n        r\"[^|]*\\|\"               # Bold header: **[F-XX] [SEVERITY] Dimension: Description**\n    2. Bold header: **[SEVERITY] Dimension**: Description\n    \"\"\"\n    findings: list[Finding] = []\n\n    # Pattern 1: **[F-XX] [SEVERITY] Dimension: Description**\n    # Pattern 2: **F-XX [SEVERITY] Dimension: Description** (variant without brackets on ID)\n    # Also matches: - **[SEVERITY] Dimension**: Description (individual reports)\n    finding_pattern = re.compile(\n        r\"[-*]*\\s*\\*\\*\"\n        r\"(?:\\[?(F-\\d+)\\]?\\s+)?\"          # Optional finding ID\n        r\"\\[(BLOCKING|WARNING|INFO)\\]\\s+\"   # Severity (required)\n        r\"([^:*]+)\"                         # Dimension\n        r\"[:\\s]*\"                           # Separator\n        r\"([^*]+)?\"                         # Description (optional inline)\n        r\"\\*\\*\",\n        re.IGNORECASE,\n    )\n\n    blocks = list(finding_pattern.finditer(section_text))\n\n    for i, block_match in enumerate(blocks):\n        block_start = block_match.end()\n        block_end = blocks[i + 1].start() if i + 1 < len(blocks) else len(section_text)\n        block_body = section_text[block_start:block_end]\n\n        finding_id = block_match.group(1) or f\"F-{len(findings) + 1:02d}\"\n        severity = block_match.group(2).upper()\n        dimension = block_match.group(3).strip().rstrip(\":\")\n        description = (block_match.group(4) or \"\").strip()\n\n        # Sub-bullet -- keep as-is\n            cleaned.append(stripped)\n        elif stripped:\n            cleaned.append(stripped)\n    return \" \".join(cleaned) if len(cleaned) <= 2 else \"\\n\".join(cleaned)\n\n\ndef _extract_files_from_location(location: str) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract file paths from a location string like 'roadmap.md:23, 359-363'.\"\"\"\n    if not location:\n        return []\n    # Match patterns like filename.ext, path/filename.ext\n    file_pattern = re.compile(r\"`?([a-zA-Z0-9_./-]+\\.[a-zA-Z0-9]+)(?::\\d+[^`]*)?`?\")\n    matches = file_pattern.findall(location)\n    # Deduplicate while preserving order\n    seen: set[str] = set()\n    result: list[str] = []\n    for f in matches:\n        if f not in seen:\n            seen.add(f)\n            result.append(f)\n    return result\n\n\ndef _validate_required_fields(\n    finding_id: str, severity: str, description: str\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Validate that required structured fields are present.\n\n    Raises ValueError when required fields are absent.\n    \"\"\"\n    missing = []\n    if not finding_id:\n        missing.append(\"id\")\n    if not severity:\n        missing.append(\"severity\")\n    if not description:\n        missing.append(\"description\")\n    if missing:\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"Required finding fields missing: {', '.join(missing)}. \"\n            \"Cannot parse finding without id, severity, and description.\"\n        )\n\n\ndef _overlay_agreement_categories(text: str, findings: list[Finding]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Overlay agreement_category from Agreement Table onto findings.\"\"\"\n    # Match Agreement Table rows: | F-XX... | ... | ... | CATEGORY |\n    table_pattern = re.compile(\n        r\"\\|\\s*(F-\\d+)[^|]*\\|\"   # Finding ID column\n        r\"[^|]*\\|\"               # Agent A or Description column\n        r\"[^|]*\\|\"               # Agent B or another column\n        r\"[^|]*\\|?\"              # Possible extra column\n        r\"\\s*(BOTH_AGREE|ONLY_A|ONLY_B|CONFLICT)\\s*\\|\",\n        re.IGNORECASE,\n    )\n    categories: dict[str, str] = {}\n    for match in table_pattern.finditer(text):\n        fid = match.group(1)\n        cat = match.group(2).upper()\n        categories[fid] = cat\n\n    for finding in findings:\n        if finding.id in categories and not finding.agreement_category:\n            finding.agreement_category = categories[finding.id]\n\n\ndef _overlay_remediation_status(text: str, findings: list[Finding]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Overlay remediation status from reflect-merged.md Agreement Table.\n\n    In reflect-merged.md format, the table has a Remediation Status column\n    with values like **FIXED**, **OUT_OF_SCOPE**, **NO_ACTION_REQUIRED**.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Look for remediation status pattern in Agreement Table rows\n    status_pattern = re.compile(\n        r\"\\|\\s*(F-\\d+)[^|]*\\|\"       # Finding ID\n        r\"[^|]*\\|[^|]*\\|[^|]*\\|\"     # Middle columns\n        r\"\\s*\\*\\*([A-Z_]+)\\*\\*\",      # Extract line numbers from locations\n    lines1 = _extract_line_numbers(f1.location)\n    lines2 = _extract_line_numbers(f2.location)\n\n    if not lines1 or not lines2:\n        # Same file but can't compare lines -- treat as match\n        return bool(files1 & files2)\n\n    # Fix guidance: merged from both reports\n\n    Non-matching findings included as-is from their source report.\n\n    This is a pure function: no I/O, no subprocess calls, no side effects.\n    \"\"\"\n    all_findings: list[Finding] = []\n    for text in report_texts:\n        try:\n            findings = _parse_flat_findings(text)\n            if not findings:\n                findings = _parse_consolidated_findings(text)\n            all_findings.extend(findings)\n        except ValueError:\n            continue\n\n    if not all_findings:\n        return []\n\n    return _deduplicate_findings(all_findings)\n\n\ndef _parse_consolidated_findings(text: str) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Extract findings from '## Consolidated Findings' sections.\"\"\"\n    # Find the Consolidated Findings section\n    match = re.search(r\"^## Consolidated Findings\\s*$\", text, re.MULTILINE)\n    if not match:\n        return []\n\n    section_text = text[match.end():]\n    # Truncate at next H2\n    next_h2 = re.search(r\"^## \", section_text, re.MULTILINE)\n    if next_h2:\n        section_text = section_text[:next_h2.start()]\n\n    return _extract_finding_blocks(section_text)\n\n\ndef _parse_flat_findings(text: str) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Extract findings from individual report '## Findings' sections.\"\"\"\n    match = re.search(r\"^## Findings\\s*$\", text, re.MULTILINE)\n    if not match:\n        return []\n\n    section_text = text[match.end():]\n    next_h2 = re.search(r\"^## \", section_text, re.MULTILINE)\n    if next_h2:\n        section_text = section_text[:next_h2.start()]\n\n    return _extract_finding_blocks(section_text)\n\n\ndef _extract_finding_blocks(section_text: str) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Extract individual finding blocks from a findings section.\n\n    Supports two patterns:\n    1. Bold header: **[F-XX] [SEVERITY] Dimension: Description**\n    2. Bold header: **[SEVERITY] Dimension**: Description\n    \"\"\"\n    findings: list[Finding] = []\n\n    # Pattern 1: **[F-XX] [SEVERITY] Dimension: Description**\n    # Pattern 2: **F-XX [SEVERITY] Dimension: Description** (variant without brackets on ID)\n    # Also matches: - **[SEVERITY] Dimension**: Description (individual reports)\n    finding_pattern = re.compile(\n        r\"[-*]*\\s*\\*\\*\"\n        r\"(?:\\[?(F-\\d+)\\]?\\s+)?\"          # Optional finding ID\n        r\"\\[(BLOCKING|WARNING|INFO)\\]\\s+\"   # Severity (required)\n        r\"([^:*]+)\"                         # Dimension\n        r\"[:\\s]*\"                           # Separator\n        r\"([^*]+)?\"                         # Description (optional inline)\n        r\"\\*\\*\",\n        re.IGNORECASE,\n    )\n\n    blocks = list(finding_pattern.finditer(section_text))\n\n    for i, block_match in enumerate(blocks):\n        block_start = block_match.end()\n        block_end = blocks[i + 1].start() if i + 1 < len(blocks) else len(section_text)\n        block_body = section_text[block_start:block_end]\n\n        finding_id = block_match.group(1) or f\"F-{len(findings) + 1:02d}\"\n        severity = block_match.group(2).upper()\n        dimension = block_match.group(3).strip().rstrip(\":\")\n        description = (block_match.group(4) or \"\").strip()\n\n        # If description is empty, use the full matched text\n        if not description:\n            description = f\"{dimension}\"\n\n        location = _extract_field(block_body, \"Location\")\n        evidence = _extract_field(block_body, \"Evidence\")\n        fix_guidance = _extract_field(block_body, \"Fix guidance\")\n        agreement_raw = _extract_field(block_body, \"Agreement\")\n        agreement = _extract_agreement_keyword(agreement_raw)\n\n        # Validate required fields\n        _validate_required_fields(finding_id, severity, description)\n\n        files_affected = _extract_files_from_location(location)\n\n        findings.append(Finding(\n            id=finding_id,\n            severity=severity,\n            dimension=dimension,\n            description=description,\n            location=location,\n            evidence=evidence,\n            fix_guidance=fix_guidance,\n            files_affected=files_affected,\n            status=\"PENDING\",\n            agreement_category=agreement,\n        ))\n\n    return findings\n\n\ndef _extract_field(body: str, field_name: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Extract a field value from a finding block body.\n\n    Handles multi-line values that continue with indentation.\n    \"\"\"\n    pattern = re.compile(\n        rf\"^\\s*-\\s+{field_name}\\s*:\\s*(.+?)(?=\\n\\s*-\\s+\\w|\\n\\s*\\n\\*\\*|\\Z)\",\n        re.MULTILINE | re.DOTALL,\n    )\n    match = pattern.search(body)\n    if not match:\n        return \"\"\n    # Clean up the extracted text\n    raw = match.group(1).strip()\n    # Collapse continuation lines\n    lines = raw.split(\"\\n\")\n    cleaned = []\n    for line in lines:\n        stripped = line.strip()\n        if stripped.startswith(\"- \") and cleaned:\n            # Sub-bullet -- keep as-is\n            cleaned.append(stripped)\n        elif stripped:\n            cleaned.append(stripped)\n    return \" \".join(cleaned) if len(cleaned) <= 2 else \"\\n\".join(cleaned)\n\n\ndef _extract_agreement_keyword(raw: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Extract agreement category keyword from raw agreement text.\n\n    E.g. 'CONFLICT (Agent A: INFO, Agent B: BLOCKING).' -> 'CONFLICT'\n    \"\"\"\n    if not raw:\n        return \"\"\n    match = re.match(r\"(BOTH_AGREE|ONLY_A|ONLY_B|CONFLICT)\", raw, re.IGNORECASE)\n    return match.group(1).upper() if match else raw\n\n\ndef _extract_files_from_location(location: str) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract file paths from a location string like 'roadmap.md:23, 359-363'.\"\"\"\n    if not location:\n        return []\n    # Match patterns like filename.ext, path/filename.ext\n    file_pattern = re.compile(r\"`?([a-zA-Z0-9_./-]+\\.[a-zA-Z0-9]+)(?::\\d+[^`]*)?`?\")\n    matches = file_pattern.findall(location)\n    # Deduplicate while preserving order\n    seen: set[str] = set()\n    result: list[str] = []\n    for f in matches:\n        if f not in seen:\n            seen.add(f)\n            result.append(f)\n    return result\n\n\ndef _validate_required_fields(\n    finding_id: str, severity: str, description: str\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Validate that required structured fields are present.\n\n    Raises ValueError when required fields are absent.\n    \"\"\"\n    missing = []\n    if not finding_id:\n        missing.append(\"id\")\n    if not severity:\n        missing.append(\"severity\")\n    if not description:\n        missing.append(\"description\")\n    if missing:\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"Required finding fields missing: {', '.join(missing)}. \"\n            \"Cannot parse finding without id, severity, and description.\"\n        )\n\n\ndef _overlay_agreement_categories(text: str, findings: list[Finding]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Overlay agreement_category from Agreement Table onto findings.\"\"\"\n    # Match Agreement Table rows: | F-XX... | ... | ... | CATEGORY |\n    table_pattern = re.compile(\n        r\"\\|\\s*(F-\\d+)[^|]*\\|\"   # Finding ID column\n        r\"[^|]*\\|\"               # Agent A or Description column\n        r\"[^|]*\\|\"               # Agent B or another column\n        r\"[^|]*\\|?\"              # Possible extra column\n        r\"\\s*(BOTH_AGREE|ONLY_A|ONLY_B|CONFLICT)\\s*\\|\",\n        re.IGNORECASE,\n    )\n    categories: dict[str, str] = {}\n    for match in table_pattern.finditer(text):\n        fid = match.group(1)\n        cat = match.group(2).upper()\n        categories[fid] = cat\n\n    for finding in findings:\n        if finding.id in categories and not finding.agreement_category:\n            finding.agreement_category = categories[finding.id]\n\n\ndef _overlay_remediation_status(text: str, findings: list[Finding]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Overlay remediation status from reflect-merged.md Agreement Table.\n\n    In reflect-merged.md format, the table has a Remediation Status column\n    with values like **FIXED**, **OUT_OF_SCOPE**, **NO_ACTION_REQUIRED**.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Look for remediation status pattern in Agreement Table rows\n    status_pattern = re.compile(\n        r\"\\|\\s*(F-\\d+)[^|]*\\|\"       # Finding ID\n        r\"[^|]*\\|[^|]*\\|[^|]*\\|\"     # Middle columns\n        r\"\\s*\\*\\*([A-Z_]+)\\*\\*\",      # Bold status value\n        re.IGNORECASE,\n    )\n    for match in status_pattern.finditer(text):\n        fid = match.group(1)\n        status_text = match.group(2).upper()\n        for finding in findings:\n            if finding.id == fid:\n                if status_text == \"FIXED\":\n                    finding.status = \"FIXED\"\n                elif status_text in (\"OUT_OF_SCOPE\", \"NO_ACTION_REQUIRED\"):\n                    finding.status = \"SKIPPED\"\n                break\n\n\ndef _deduplicate_findings(findings: list[Finding]) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Deduplicate findings using two-step rule from spec §8/OQ-003.\n\n    Step 1: Location match -- same file + within 5 lines = candidate duplicate\n    Step 2: Severity resolution -- higher severity wins; fix_guidance merged\n    \"\"\"\n    if not findings:\n        return []\n\n    result: list[Finding] = []\n    merged_indices: set[int] = set()\n\n    for i, f1 in enumerate(findings):\n        if i in merged_indices:\n            continue\n\n        best = f1\n        for j, f2 in enumerate(findings):\n            if j <= i or j in merged_indices:\n                continue\n\n            if _is_location_match(f1, f2):\n                merged_indices.add(j)\n                best = _merge_findings(best, f2)\n\n        result.append(best)\n\n    return result\n\n\ndef _is_location_match(f1: Finding, f2: Finding) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if two findings refer to the same file within 5 lines.\"\"\"\n    files1 = set(f1.files_affected)\n    files2 = set(f2.files_affected)\n    if not files1 or not files2:\n        return False\n    if not files1 & files2:\n        return False\n\n    # Extract line numbers from locations\n    lines1 = _extract_line_numbers(f1.location)\n    lines2 = _extract_line_numbers(f2.location)\n\n    if not lines1 or not lines2:\n        # Same file but can't compare lines -- treat as match\n        return bool(files1 & files2)\n\n    # Check if any line pair is within 5 lines\n    for l1 in lines1:\n        for l2 in lines2:\n            if abs(l1 - l2) <= 5:\n                return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef _extract_line_numbers(location: str) -> list[int]:\n    \"\"\"Extract line numbers from a location string.\"\"\"\n    # Match patterns like :23, :359-363\n    line_pattern = re.compile(r\":(\\d+)(?:-(\\d+))?\")\n    numbers: list[int] = []\n    for match in line_pattern.finditer(location):\n        numbers.append(int(match.group(1)))\n        if match.group(2):\n            numbers.append(int(match.group(2)))\n    return numbers\n\n\ndef _merge_findings(f1: Finding, f2: Finding) -> Finding:\n    \"\"\"Merge two duplicate findings. Higher severity wins; guidance merged.\"\"\"\n    rank1 = _SEVERITY_RANK.get(f1.severity, 0)\n    rank2 = _SEVERITY_RANK.get(f2.severity, 0)\n\n    winner = f1 if rank1 >= rank2 else f2\n    loser = f2 if rank1 >= rank2 else f1\n\n    # Merge fix guidance\n    merged_guidance = winner.fix_guidance\n    if loser.fix_guidance and loser.fix_guidance != winner.fix_guidance:\n        merged_guidance = f\"{winner.fix_guidance}\\n[Additional]: {loser.fix_guidance}\"\n\n    # Merge files_affected\n    all_files = list(dict.fromkeys(winner.files_affected + loser.files_affected))\n\n    return Finding(\n        id=winner.id,\n        severity=winner.severity,\n        dimension=winner.dimension,\n        description=winner.description,\n        location=winner.location,\n        evidence=winner.evidence,\n        fix_guidance=merged_guidance,\n        files_affected=all_files,\n        status=\"PENDING\",\n        agreement_category=winner.agreement_category,\n    )\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":265,"oldLines":7,"newStart":265,"newLines":7,"lines":["         categories[fid] = cat"," ","     for finding in findings:","-        if finding.id in categories and not finding.agreement_category:","+        if finding.id in categories:","             finding.agreement_category = categories[finding.id]"," "," "]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}
